<name>Phillip Rogers</name><Time>1533398164866<//Time><Rate>5< /Rate>< Review>
I brought my 2001 CBR929RR in to the shop for a full rebuild. New plastics, fork seals, chain, wheel bearings, valve adjustment, and electrical work. They were upfront about the wait time and possible costs. The kicker was half the bike was in a box. Tom the mechanic assigned to the job used to have a 929RR and really did a great job putting it back together and getting it loud and fast again. I would definitely recommend them due to the fact that they did everything the right way. They could have cut corners on certain things, but they ordered the missing parts and sorted out some problems. The only down fall was how anxious I was to get the bike back after I stopped by the shop to drop off some parts and check out the progress. They came in way under my budget and didn't try to nickel and dime me. For as long as I'm in the area they get my business. Again, much appreciated guys!</Review>

< text>
Pros: Clean facility, good value, security, and very very friendly staff

Facility has external gates that are only open during storage hours followed by gates and security locked elevators- you are given a code and you can only access your floor.

Staff are very friendly and willing to help in any way possible. I can't say enough good things about them- if you need a storage, stop by and see it for yourself. Joe is great!

Value: their pricing i believe is on par with the market rate, they do offer specials so it doesn't hurt to ask. But with all that you get, I think this place is worth it.

Con: can't think of any

Overall, when I was searching for a storage, I called around for rates and availability. There were some that were nationally ran where the call center was in some other state and their sole goal was to make the sales. When I called Los Angeles Self Storage, someone actually picked up the call, gave me the breakdown, provided me with directions and when I got there, they walked around to show me the storage itself. Everything went very smoothly and on-site staff were on point with their customer service.  All this was actually at a lower monthly rate than other places I called. So, they definitely earn 5 stars and I hope you will check it out for yourself!</text>
